# If you manually edit this file, please be make sure know those
# tags meaning and update with those tags if needed. Otherwise
# your edit may be overrided during next syntax auto upgrade.
#
# Tag Usage:
# [bt]/[bd] - branchpt/buildno.
# [md] - model/platform list
# [og] - original object/attr type.
# [od] - override default value exist.
# [ot] - override objlimit exist.
# [ud] - user defined default-values/objects/records.
# [ut] - user defined objlimit.
# [uo] - user defined options.
# [ua] - user defined objects/attributes.
# [fg] - flags
# [sz] - string attribute maximum length.
# [lmt] - integer attribute minimum & maximum value.
# [opt] - option/multiopt attribute options.
# [xs] - apply/no-apply XSS check.
# [rd] - objects/attributes are readonly.
# [hd] - objects/attributes are hidden.
# [ug] - objects/attributes are orphaned and not-supported.
# [un] - attributes force show unset command.
# [nv] - objects/attributes no verify when install.
# [nd] - no default value for attributes. always show up.
# [mc] - multiple int/string duplicate checking (by default).
# [+R] - reserved record is read-only.
# [+D] - reserved record can be deleted (should useless).
# [+H] - reserved record is hidden & read-only object.
# [nat] - nat only objects.
# [tp] - tp only objects.
# [-ut] - do not auto set tag[ut].
# [-un] - do not auto set tag[un].
# [+ug] - do not auto delete tag[ug] by raw syntax files.
# [+rd] - do not auto delete tag[rd] by raw syntax files.
# [+xs] - do not auto delete tag[xs] by raw syntax files.
# [-mc] - do not perform multiple int/string dup checking.
# [mu] - same as FGT flag PARSE_F_MUST.
# [+mu] - attribute MUST have a value.
# [+nd] - do not auto delete tag[nd] by raw syntax files.
# [ndg] - no default value for global adom.
#
# Macro Usage:
# [@a_fgt] - all Fortigate models.
# [@a_foc] - all FortiCarrier models.
# [@a_fwf] - all FortiWiFi models.
# [@f_xxx] - all models that have feature f_xxx.
